   <div class="title_area" style="background: url(http://travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Kruger-National-Park-2014/i-NtVPLh9/0/X3/GMA_0250-X3.jpg) no-repeat center center; background-size: cover; margin-top: -163px; padding-top: 173px;">
    <div class="title-meta">
     <div class="container">
      <div class="sixteen columns alpha omega">
       <h1>
        2014: A Year In Photography
       </h1>
       <p>
        <i class="fa fa-calendar">
        </i>
        Posted: January 2, 2015
        <i class="fa fa-tags">
        </i>
        Categories:
        <a href="http://everything-everywhere.com/category/photo-essay/" rel="category tag">
         Photo Essay
        </a>
       </p>

     </div>

    <div class="sixteen columns alpha omega">
     <article class="post-21476 post type-post status-publish format-standard hentry category-photo-essay" id="post-21476">
      <section class="entry">
       <aside class="mashsb-container">

       <p>
        2014 was another landmark year for me in terms of travel and photography.
       </p>
       <ul>
        <li>
         In February, I was named the
         <strong>
          Travel Photographer of the Year
         </strong>
         by the
         <a href="http://www.natja.org/awards/2013-winners" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://www.natja.org/awards/2013-winners', 'North American Travel Journalists Association']);" target="_blank">
          North American Travel Journalists Association
         </a>
         .
        </li>
        <li>
         In April, I was named the
         <strong>
          Travel Photographer of the Year
         </strong>
         by the
         <a href="http://satw.org/centralstates/2014-central-states-writing-and-photography-winners/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://satw.org/centralstates/2014-central-states-writing-and-photography-winners/', 'Central States Chapter of the Society of American Travel Writers']);" target="_blank">
          Central States Chapter of the Society of American Travel Writers
         </a>
         .
        </li>
        <li>
         In April I also took the
         <strong>
          Gold Medal
         </strong>
         in the annual
         <a href="http://en-corporate.canada.travel/content/ctc_news/northern-lights-awards-2013-san-francisco" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://en-corporate.canada.travel/content/ctc_news/northern-lights-awards-2013-san-francisco', 'Northern Lights Awards by the Canadian Tourism Commission']);" target="_blank">
          Northern Lights Awards by the Canadian Tourism Commission
         </a>
         for photojournalism of Canada.
        </li>
        <li>
         In September, I was runner up in the
         <strong>
          Travel Photographer of the Year
         </strong>
         competition for the
         <a href="http://satw.org/muster2015/poty_silver/index.html" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://satw.org/muster2015/poty_silver/index.html', 'Society of American Travel writers']);" target="_blank">
          Society of American Travel writers
         </a>
         .
        </li>
        <li>
         In September, I also won a
         <a href="http://satwf.com/2014_SATW_Foundation_Lowell_Thomas_Travel_Jour_(1)/2014_List_of_Winners" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://satwf.com/2014_SATW_Foundation_Lowell_Thomas_Travel_Jour_(1)/2014_List_of_Winners', 'Lowell Thomas Award in Photo Illustration of Travel']);" target="_blank">
          Lowell Thomas Award in Photo Illustration of Travel
         </a>
         . My
         <strong>
          3rd Lowell Thomas Award
         </strong>
         in as many years.
        </li>
       </ul>
       <p>
        All-in-all, not a bad year.
       </p>
       <p>
        Here are some of my favorite photo of 2014. I hope you enjoy viewing them as much as I did taking them! You can also go back view my
        <a href="http://everything-everywhere.studionashvegas.com/2014/01/02/2013-year-photos/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://everything-everywhere.studionashvegas.com/2014/01/02/2013-year-photos/', '2013']);" target="_blank">
         2013
        </a>
        and
        <a href="http://everything-everywhere.studionashvegas.com/2012/12/28/photo-essay-2012-travels-through-photos/" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://everything-everywhere.studionashvegas.com/2012/12/28/photo-essay-2012-travels-through-photos/', '2012']);" target="_blank">
         2012
        </a>
        photography retrospectives.
        <br/>
        <span id="more-21476">
        </span>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Australia/New-South-Wales/Sydney-Fireworks-2014/i-LS9GdGJ/1/1200x1200/GMA_0956-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
       </p>
       <p>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [1]
        </span>
        2014 began with a bang for me as I was in Sydney to photograph their annual New Years Fireworks on the Sydney Harbor. I would love to return to photograph the fireworks again, as I wasnt able to set up at an ideal spot.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Drakensberg-Park-2014/i-NDhFZcV/0/1200x1200/GMA_1271-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [2]
        </span>
        I spent the first half of the year in Africa. I started my African adventure in the city of Durban where I was headquartered for a few weeks. During my time, I visited nearby Drakensberg National Park and drove up the Sani Pass to Lesotho.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/ISimangaliso-Wetland-Park-2014/i-vpzDRDg/0/1200x1200/GMA_1703%202-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [3]
        </span>
        After Durban, I did a road trip through northern South Africa, Swaziland and Botswana. During my trip I stopped in iSimangaliso Wetlands Park where I captured this image of young male hippos sparring with each other.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Mapungubwe-2014/i-7VTh9xB/0/1200x1200/GMA_2074-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [4]
        </span>
        The northernmost point of my road trip was Mapungubwe National Park. This photo shows the Limpopo River and three different countries: South Africa, Zimbabwe and Botswana.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Zimbabwe/Victoria-Falls-2014/i-dPM83SD/0/1200x1200/GMA_2154-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [5]
        </span>
        I ended my road trip in Johannesburg and met my friend Shannon ODonnell. We flew up to Victoria Falls in Zimbabwe/Zambia and experienced the thunder of falls at almost the high water mark.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Atlantic/St-Helena/St-Helena-2014/i-kQjgsnW/0/1200x1200/GMA_3234-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [6]
        </span>
        After visiting Victoria Falls and driving down to Cape Town from Johannesburg, I hopped on a royal mail ship for an 18 day round trip voyage to the remote island of St. Helena. Most famous as the place where Napoleon was exiled, it was an amazing place in its own right. This is the Lots Wife rock formation on the island.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Atlantic/St-Helena/St-Helena-2014/i-kF9mCjK/0/1200x1200/GMA_3051-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [7]
        </span>
        In the capital of St. Helena, Jamestown, there is a 699 step staircase which goes up the side of a cliff. Needless to say, driving is much easier than walking.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Cape-Town-2014/i-3br68tj/0/1200x1200/GMA_2769-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [8]
        </span>
        After returning to Cape Town from St Helena, I had 2 weeks to explore the city before my next adventure. I found Cape Town to be not only my favorite city in Africa, but one of the best cities in the world.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Cape-Town-2014/i-qf6PLZH/0/1200x1200/GMA_2879-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [9]
        </span>
        The most iconic part of Cape Town is of course Table Mountain. Ive been to the top several times and the view is really hit or miss depending on the weather. Thankfully I was able to visit once this year on a very clear day.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Namibia/Luderitz-2014/i-xdQNRLF/0/1200x1200/GMA_4215-1-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [10]
        </span>
        In early April I began my biggest adventure of the year. I sailed up the west coast of Africa with
        <a href="http://gadventures.com" onclick="_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'outbound-article', 'http://gadventures.com', 'G Adventures']);" target="_blank">
         G Adventures
        </a>
        . (
        <a href="http://photoessay.everything-everywhere.com/sailing-up-west-africa" target="_blank">
         see my full photo essay here
        </a>
        ). Our first stop was Luderitz, Namibia which is home to the Kolmanskop ghost town. There, the desert is slowly reclaiming the buildings.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Angola/Lobito-2014/i-5RrnxSK/0/1200x1200/GMA_4710-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [11]
        </span>
        After a stop in Swakopmund and Walvis Bay, Namibia, our next stop was in Lobito and Benguela, Angola. Not a country which gets many visitors, we did a tour of both cities and also watch some street musicians perform.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="aligncenter" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Repbulic-of-Congo/Point-Noire-2014/i-DRZsg39/0/1200x1200/GMA_4967-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [12]
        </span>
        After Angola we sailed to Port Noire in the Republic of Congo. Again, it is a place which doesnt get a lot of visitors. The highlight of the trip was delivering school supplies to a local school and being treated to a singing performance by the children.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Sao-Tome-and-Principe/Sao-Tome-2014/i-2Gj9h9c/0/1200x1200/GMA_5507-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [13]
        </span>
        From Port Noire we crossed the equator and visited the island of Sao Tome, capital of the country of Sao Tome and Principe. Given how small the island is, we were able to see quite a bit of it. The highlight for me was visiting the Delmonte Coffee Plantation and photographing some of the local kids there.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Sao-Tome-and-Principe/Principe-2014/i-tttFpct/0/1200x1200/GMA_6183-1-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [14]
        </span>
        Our visit to the island of Principe was mostly a day of relaxing. While I was there I went exploring with one of the boat staff and found this abandoned church out in the forest.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Togo/Lome-2014/i-4gjfRzt/0/1200x1200/GMA_6502.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [15]
        </span>
        After being denied a landing in Benin due to the port being closed for Easter, we changed plans on the fly and visited Lome, Togo for Easter instead. There we visited the village of Akato Viepe where we were treated to a royal reception.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Benin/Cotonou-2014/i-vkR6tnG/0/1200x1200/GMA_6928-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [16]
        </span>
        In Benin we visited the village of Ganvie. Originally founded several hundred years ago by people who fled to the middle of a lake to escape slavers, the village still exists today.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Ghana/Takoradi-2014/i-65Gdj4K/0/1200x1200/GMA_7111-Edit-1-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [17]
        </span>
        In Ghana, we visited several slave castles along the coast along with the capital of Accra. This photos is of fishermen getting their ships ready to go out in the town of Cape Coast, Ghana.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Sierra-Leone/Freetown-2014/i-xSQg4SG/0/1200x1200/GMA_7909-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [18]
        </span>
        Perhaps the most photogenic place we visited in West Africa was Sierra Leone. Despite all the bad press which the country gets, I found the people to be very friendly and outgoing. We anchored in Freetown for two nights.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Sierra-Leone/Freetown-2014/i-ZN6Cwxm/0/1200x1200/GMA_7577-Edit-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [19]
        </span>
        We had the Sierra Leone national Dance Troupe come and perform for us on the ship. During the performance, I got this shot of a fire dancer, which is one of my favorite photos of the year.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="473" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Sierra-Leone/Freetown-2014/i-R3QTCjz/0/1200x1200/GMA_7870-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [20]
        </span>
        I met these kids near John Obey beach and they were just delightful. They would ask me to lift them up on the branch of the tree, and then jump off. All the while, they wanted me to take their photo and I happily obliged.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/The-Gambia/Banjul-2014/i-VKQSzNN/0/1200x1200/GMA_8120-1-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [22]
        </span>
        As we left Sierra Leone, we left the very warm waters of the Gulf of Guinea and turned the corner and started heading north. We arrived in Banjul, The Gambia. An interesting country and city, totally surrounded by Senegal by land. I took this photo of a woman selling fish in the main market in Banjul.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Senegal/Dakkar-2014/i-7jFpKDT/0/1200x1200/GMA_8351-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [23]
        </span>
        Dakkar is very different from the rest of West Africa we had just visited. A more modern and cosmopolitan city, it was easy to see the French influences despite all the traffic and commotion.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Senegal/Dakkar-2014/i-P7QQnb5/0/1200x1200/GMA_8419_20_21_22_23_tonemapped-Edit-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [24]
        </span>
        There are many Doors of No Return in Africa. Doors where slaves left to board ships, never to return. This one on Goree Island draws many visitors and students who come to learn about history of slavery in the region.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/Western-Sahara/Dakhla-2014/i-DB7Fhsm/0/1200x1200/GMA_8941-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [25]
        </span>
        As we moved north, we visited the Moroccan controlled area of Western Sahara. I had no idea what to expect before I arrived, and was surprised to learn that Dakhla was one of the kite surfing capitals of the world.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Spain/Fuerteventura-2014/i-dLDRNdF/0/1200x1200/GMA_9125-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [26]
        </span>
        Our last stop before arriving in Morocco was the island of Fuerteventura in the Canary Islands. I had previously visit almost all of the Canary Islands back in 2011.except for Fuerteventura. All the islands are different and the sand dunes of Fuerteventura proved that true again.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Cape-Town-2014/i-d44tBcf/0/1200x1200/GMA_9398-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [27]
        </span>
        After sailing up the entire length of the African continent from Cape Town I flew..back to Cape Town! Here I met the photographers who were attending my 3rd annual photography tour with G Adventures. One of the first stops on the photography tour was Cape Point, where we saw an odd site: a rare cape zebra foraging in the ash of a fire. It looked like he was in the middle of snow!
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Cape-Town-2014/i-CpZQGts/0/1200x1200/GMA_9278-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [28]
        </span>
        The beach in the nearby town of Muizenberg has some amazingly colorful beach houses.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Kruger-National-Park-2014/i-7qKfFq9/0/1200x1200/GMA_0848-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [29]
        </span>
        The high point of the photography tour was Kruger National Park. We spent two days in the park photographing the wildlife in the area. On the second day in the park, we saw all five of the Big Five before lunch! This leopard sitting in a tree was the one which completed the Big Five for us.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="636" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Africa/South-Africa/Kruger-National-Park-2014/i-bPrJthS/0/1200x1200/GMA_1250-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [30]
        </span>
        The sheer number of large animals in Kruger was something I had never seen before. You were almost never more than 10-15 minutes away from seeing something large and unforgettable.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Atlantic/Bermuda/Bermuda-2014/i-R9CG6xM/0/1200x1200/GMA_1750-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [31]
        </span>
        After I left Africa I returned to the US and had some business meetings in Toronto and New York. I had a few days downtime so I flew to Bermuda, an island I hadnt visited before.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Michigan/Isle-Royale-National-Park-2014/i-GhF8Cc6/0/1200x1200/GMA_2044-Edit-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [32]
        </span>
        After a few weeks of rest, I set out on my longest adventure of the year. A 3-month, 12,000 mile road trip through the western United States and Canada photographing national parks. This photo is of the Rock of Ages Lighthouse in Isle Royale National Park, Michigan.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Minnesota/Voyageurs-National-Park-2014/i-Fn7xsbx/0/1200x1200/GMA_2164-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [33]
        </span>
        My next park was Voyagers National Park in Northern Minnesota. Heavy rains and flooding made for some interesting photo opportunities.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Manitoba/Riding-Mountain-National-Park/i-G4LLKw3/0/1200x1200/GMA_2482-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [34]
        </span>
        Riding Mountain National Park in Manitoba is about 2 hours from Winnipeg. It is a lesser known national park, but is a great place to visit when in Manitoba.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Saskatchewan/Grasslands-National-Park-2014/i-7rn4c8M/0/1200x1200/GMA_2720-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [35]
        </span>
        The drive through the Great Plains wasnt a boring one for me. Ive always loved the prairie and I was looking forward to visiting Grasslands National Park. Saskatchewan was also my 10th and final Canadian province to visit.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Alberta/Waterton-Lakes-National-Park/i-Q5DSQmW/0/1200x1200/GMA_3431-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [36]
        </span>
        Waterton Lakes National Park on the southern border of Alberta surrounds a beautiful lake. It is also the home of the famous Prince of Wales Hotel, one of the great Canadian lodges.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="669" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Alberta/Calgary-Stampede-2014/i-zhCJxdj/0/1200x1200/_GMA9163-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [37]
        </span>
        I had a blast photographing the Calgary Stampede, the worlds largest rodeo. The action was so fast paced, that an award winning shot could happen at any moment.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="659" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Alberta/Banff-National-Park-2014/i-JNvTsQj/0/1200x1200/GMA_7777-Edit-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [38]
        </span>
        I was so happy to return to Banff. It is truly a photographers playground. The view of Moraine Lake in the morning is one of the iconic images of the Canadian Rockies.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Alberta/Jasper-National-Park-2014/i-6hwZ2Bj/0/1200x1200/GMA_8078-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [39]
        </span>
        In Jasper National Park I had the chance to get some great lightning shots. It is something i dont often have the opportunity to do, but there was a storm coming over the mountains just as the sun was setting, and the effect was dramatic.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Alberta/Wood-Buffalo-National-Park-201/i-6q2xhdR/0/1200x1200/GMA_8705-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [40]
        </span>
        Wood Buffalo National Park is the 2nd largest national park in the world, and one of the least visited in North America. A massive 44,807 km
        <sup>
         2
        </sup>
        (17,300 mi
        <sup>
         2
        </sup>
        ) area in northern Alberta and southern Northwest Territories, it is a landscape of forest, lakes, meadows and wetlands, parts of which have never been visited by humans.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Northwest-Territories/Nahanni-National-Park-2014/i-WBGPC34/0/1200x1200/GMA_9530-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [41]
        </span>
        I have been to a lot of places all over the world, and I can say without hesitation that Nahanni National Park is one of the greatest. Unfortunately, it is also one of the most difficult to visit. First, you have to get yourself to Fort Simpson, NWT. Then you need to get on a float plane, as the park has no roads. Only 800 people a year get to see the awesome grandeur which is Nahanni. Virginia Falls in Nahanni is one of the largest waterfalls in the world, yet few people even know it exists.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/Northwest-Territories/Nahanni-National-Park-2014/i-H9xzpLn/0/1200x1200/GMA_9786-Edit-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [42]
        </span>
        One benefit to taking a float plane into the park is that you get great aerial views of the surrounding mountains. Nahanni has parts which will remind you of Yellowstone, the Grand Canyon and Yosemite.all in one place.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="665" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/British-Columbia/Northern-Rocky-Mountains-2014/i-hZCKm6H/1/1200x1200/GMA_0401-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [43]
        </span>
        I came south through British Columbia and photographed some of the Northern Rockies. I got this shot of a moose that had been feeding underwater from a canoe.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="669" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/British-Columbia/Northern-Rocky-Mountains-2014/i-tTtP6sV/0/1200x1200/_GMA9564-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [44]
        </span>
        I have wanted to get some decent photos of bald eagles for years, but never had the right equipment and circumstances. At the WAC Bennet Dam in British Columbia, I had both and finally was able to get some bald eagle photos I could be proud of.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/British-Columbia/Yoho-National-Park-2014/i-c9J3ft3/0/1200x1200/GMA_1011-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [45]
        </span>
        Yoho National Park is on the British Columbia side of the Rocky Mountains, adjacent to Banff and Kootenay National Parks. It his home to Takakkaw Falls, one of the highest waterfalls in Canada.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/North-America/British-Columbia/Pacific-Rim-National-Park-2014/i-hqj445t/0/1200x1200/GMA_1248-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [46]
        </span>
        Pacific Rim National Park is the on the wild Pacific coast of Canada. The thick fog that I experienced when I was there was totally gone once I went just a mile inland. It was incredible to see just how much the weather changed once you get near the ocean.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/MexicoandCentralAmerica/Mexico/Chichen-Itza-2014/i-JCC5SkZ/0/1200x1200/GMA_1821-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [47]
        </span>
        In September I attended a conference in Cancun and made it a point to finally go and visit Chichen Itza. It is one of the New Seven Wonders of the world and it was well worth the trip.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Ireland/Ireland-2014/i-hJLdjmw/0/1200x1200/GMA_2067-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [48]
        </span>
        I returned to Ireland in 2014, which is never a bad thing. This year I explored parts of the Wild Atlantic Way before heading to a conference.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Malta/Valletta-2014/i-FvTVKnd/0/1200x1200/GMA_2961-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [49]
        </span>
        After Ireland, I visited Malta for the first time. This image was taken in the capital of Valletta at the Saluting Battery. Every day at noon they fire a cannon, as was the tradition so ships could set their clocks.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Cyprus/Cyprus-2014/i-mQDH3sv/0/1200x1200/GMA_3154-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [50]
        </span>
        After Malta I flew to Cyprus to meet up with some old friends and visit the World Heritage sites on the island. The Painted churches of the Troodos Region was a especially nice. I ended up visiting 5 of the 10 churches which comprised the world heritage site and was able to take photos in a few of them. The churches are all very small and date back over 500 years.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Greece/Meteora-2014/i-NdkJkjv/0/1200x1200/GMA_3931-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [51]
        </span>
        After a conference in Athens, I was going to head north to Serbia, but I was forced to change plans and ended up going to Meteora. Im glad I did. It is an amazing environment and a wonderful place to photograph.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/England/Jurassic-Coast-2014/i-hPC92tH/0/1200x1200/GMA_4569-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [52]
        </span>
        I had one final conference to attend in London in November. After which I headed south to Cornwall and Devon to visit some world heritage sites I hadnt been to in England. One of which was the Jurassic Coast.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <p>
        <img class="alignnone" height="664" src="//travelphotos.everything-everywhere.com/Europe/Spain/Girona-201415/i-tQdSFZm/0/1200x1200/GMA_4893-1200x1200.jpg" width="1200"/>
        <br/>
        <span class="dropcap">
         [53]
        </span>
        After all the travel Id done this year I needed to take a break, so I spent the last month and a half of 2014 in Girona, Catalonia. Despite resting and getting some work done, I have still and time to go out and shoot.
        <br/>
        <br clear="all"/>
       </p>
       <hr/>
       <div class="ctx-clearfix" id="ctx-sl-subscribe">
       </div>
       <div class="ctx-module-container ctx-clearfix" id="ctx-module">
       </div>
      </section>

       <div class="single-comment clearfix" id="comment-88659">
        <div class="comment-author vcard">

         <p>
          Holy crap, youre influential.   Youre work may be important, but I think youll agree that it lacks the kind of irreverent silliness that youll find in our four wee videos explaining our jihad against boring photography.  Theyre on the Visual Conservancy Facebook page.   Were a group of photographers whose spiritual home is Stillwater, Minnesota.

		function execDelayedScripts(){
			if (scriptsToLoad&lt;=0){
				for (var i = 0; i &lt; asyncFunctions.length; i++){
					asyncFunctions[i]();
				}
			}else{
				setTimeout(execDelayedScripts,100);
			}
		}

		function loadAsyncScript(script){
			if (typeof(script.deps) == 'object'){
				for (var i = 0; i &lt; script.deps.length; i++){
					if (!include(loadedScripts,script.deps[i])){

						setTimeout(function (){
							loadAsyncScript(script);
						},100);
						return;
					}
				}
			}
			if (script.extra!=''){
				var extra = document.createElement("script");
				extra.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
				extra.innerHTML = script.extra;
				document.body.appendChild(extra);
			}


			if (script.src!=''){
				var element = document.createElement("script");
				element.setAttribute('type','text/javascript');
				element.src = decodeURIComponent(script.src.replace(/\+/g, ' '));

				onload(element,function(){
					scriptsToLoad--;
					loadedScripts.push(script.name);
				});

				document.body.appendChild(element);
			}else{
				scriptsToLoad--;
				loadedScripts.push(script.name);
			}
		}

		var include = Array.prototype.indexOf
			?
				function(arr, obj) { return arr.indexOf(obj) !== -1; }
			:
				function(arr, obj) {
					for(var i = -1, j = arr.length; ++i &lt; j;)
					if(arr[i] === obj) return true;
					return false;
				};

		scriptsToLoad =  asyncScripts.length;
		for (var i = 0; i &lt; asyncScripts.length; i++){
			loadAsyncScript(asyncScripts[i]);
		}

		function documentReady() {
			execDelayedScripts();
		}

		function onload(element,func){
			if (element.addEventListener){
				element.addEventListener("load", func, false);
			}else if (element.attachEvent){
				element.attachEvent("onload", func);
			}else{
				element.onload = func;
			}
		}

		onload(window,documentReady);
  </script>
